USERMESSAGE #10
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→# OhMyDoc — QA Regression Suite
     2→
     3→Playwright end-to-end tests for [OhMyDoc](https://ohmydoc.vercel.app), an AI-powered document formatter.
     4→
     5→## What's tested
     6→
     7→| Group | Scenarios |
     8→|-------|-----------|
     9→| **1. Basic Load** | Page title, textarea visible, Format button disabled when empty, placeholder text, no console errors, button enables with sufficient input |
    10→| **2. Happy Path — Resume** | Full resume formatting flow, loading state, preview, no raw XML tags, content preservation, HTML structure in output |
    11→| **3. Happy Path — Cover Letter** | Cover letter formatting, content verification |
    12→| **4. Mutation Warning** | DOM inspection for divergence/mutation warning elements, formatted content assertion |
    13→| **5. PDF Export** | Export button disabled before formatting, enabled after, `window.print()` triggered |
    14→| **6. Validation** | Empty and short input keep Format button disabled |
    15→| **7. Skeleton Loading** | Shimmer appears during load, disappears on completion |
    16→| **8. Sample Content** | Sample content availability (button or placeholder), formatting of sample-like content |
    17→
    18→**Total: 16 tests** across 8 feature areas (test 8b skips automatically when no dedicated sample button is present).
    19→
    20→## Requirements
    21→
    22→- Node.js 18+
    23→- Chromium (installed automatically by Playwright)
    24→
    25→## Setup
    26→
    27→```bash
    28→npm install
    29→npx playwright install chromium
    30→```
    31→
    32→## Running tests
    33→
    34→```bash
    35→# Run all tests
    36→npm test
    37→
    38→# Run with visible browser
    39→npx playwright test --headed
    40→
    41→# Run a specific test group
    42→npx playwright test --grep "8"
    43→
    44→# Open HTML report after a run
    45→npm run test:report
    46→```
    47→
    48→## Configuration
    49→
    50→Tests run against `https://ohmydoc.vercel.app` by default.
    51→
    52→Override with the `BASE_URL` environment variable:
    53→
    54→```bash
    55→BASE_URL=https://staging.ohmydoc.vercel.app npx playwright test
    56→```
    57→
    58→Or create a `.env` file:
    59→
    60→```
    61→BASE_URL=https://ohmydoc.vercel.app
    62→```
    63→
    64→## CI notes
    65→
    66→- GitHub Actions workflow at `.github/workflows/ci.yml` — runs on push, PR, and weekly schedule
    67→- Tests run serially (1 worker) — the AI formatting API must not be rate-limited by parallel calls
    68→- AI-dependent tests use a 90s timeout with fast-fail on API errors
    69→- `test.slow()` is set on tests that involve AI calls (expected ~10–20s each)
    70→- Screenshots are saved on failure under `test-results/`
    71→- HTML report is saved as a CI artifact under `playwright-report/`
    72→- Override the target URL via the `BASE_URL` repository variable in GitHub Actions
    73→
    74→## Known observations
    75→
    76→- **No "Load Sample" button**: Sample content is shown as textarea placeholder text only. Test 8b skips cleanly; tests 8a/8c adapt accordingly. A dedicated "Try Sample" button would improve first-visit UX.
    77→- **Mutation warning**: A divergence banner appears after formatting (observed in test 4) — this is expected behavior when AI rewrites content significantly (>5% divergence).
    78→- **Error phrase detection**: `waitForFormattingOutcome` only fast-fails on API key configuration phrases, not generic words like "error" or "failed", to avoid false positives on normal UI text.
    79→

    67→// ─── Helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    68→
    69→async function getTextarea(page: Page) {
    70→  return page.locator('textarea');
    71→}
    72→
    73→/**
    74→ * Reliably fill a textarea and wait for Vue's reactive model to update.
    75→ * Uses click + fill + value verification to avoid intermittent fill() issues.
    76→ */
    77→async function fillTextarea(page: Page, text: string): Promise<void> {
    78→  const textarea = page.locator('textarea');
    79→  await textarea.click();
    80→  await textarea.fill(text);
    81→  // Wait for Vue reactivity to process the input event
    82→  await page.waitForTimeout(300);
    83→  // Verify the value was actually set
    84→  const value = await textarea.inputValue();
    85→  if (value.length < 10 && text.length > 10) {
    86→    // Retry once if fill didn't work
    87→    await textarea.click();
    88→    await textarea.fill(text);
    89→    await page.waitForTimeout(500);
    90→  }
    91→}
    92→
    93→async function getFormatButton(page: Page) {
    94→  return page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i });
    95→}
    96→
    97→/**
    98→ * Returns the sample content button/link if the product provides one.
    99→ * OhMyDoc currently shows sample content in the textarea placeholder only;
   100→ * a dedicated button would be the preferred UX pattern.
   101→ */
   102→async function getSampleButton(page: Page) {
   103→  return page.getByRole('button', { name: /sample/i })
   104→    .or(page.getByRole('link', { name: /sample/i }))
   105→    .or(page.getByText(/try sample|load sample|use sample|sample resume/i));
   106→}
   107→
   108→/**
   109→ * Wait for AI formatting to complete OR for an error state to appear.
   110→ * Returns 'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'.
   111→ * Uses a short-circuit: if error text appears within 15s we don't wait 90s.
   112→ * @param successText Optional text to look for in the preview to confirm success.
   113→ *                    Defaults to 'Alex Rivera'. Pass null to use generic detection.
   114→ */
   115→async function waitForFormattingOutcome(
   116→  page: Page,
   117→  successText: string | null = 'Alex Rivera'
   118→): Promise<'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'> {
   119→  const deadline = Date.now() + 90_000;
   120→  // Keep phrases specific to real API configuration errors, not generic UI words
   121→  const errorPhrases = [
   122→    'api key is not configured',
   123→    'api key not configured',
   124→    'openai api key',
   125→    'not configured',
   126→  ];
   127→
   128→  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
   129→    // Check for success
   130→    if (successText) {
   131→      const textVisible = await page.getByText(successText, { exact: false }).isVisible().catch(() => false);
   132→      if (textVisible) return 'success';
   133→    } else {
   134→      // Generic check: placeholder gone + Format button back to idle state
   135→      const placeholderGone = !(await page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.').isVisible().catch(() => true));
   136→      const btnIdle = await page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i }).isVisible().catch(() => false);
   137→      if (placeholderGone && btnIdle) return 'success';
   138→    }
   139→
   140→    // Check for API error fast
   141→    const bodyText = (await page.locator('body').innerText().catch(() => '')).toLowerCase();
   142→    if (errorPhrases.some(phrase => bodyText.includes(phrase))) {
   143→      return 'api_error';
   144→    }
   145→
   146→    await page.waitForTimeout(1000);
   147→  }
   148→  return 'timeout';
   149→}
   150→

   152→

   181→  page.on('console', msg => {
   182→    if (msg.type() === 'error') errors.push(msg.text());
   183→  });
   184→  await page.goto(BASE_URL);
   185→  await page.waitForLoadState('networkidle');

   187→    !e.includes('favicon') &&
   188→    !e.includes('net::ERR') &&
   189→    !e.includes('ERR_BLOCKED') &&
   190→    !e.includes('extension')

   212→// ─── 2. Happy Path — Resume ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   213→
   214→test('2. Happy path — resume formatting', async ({ page }) => {
   215→  test.slow();
   216→  await page.goto(BASE_URL);
   217→
   218→  await fillTextarea(page, RESUME_TEXT);
   219→
   220→  const formatBtn = await getFormatButton(page);
   221→  await expect(formatBtn).toBeEnabled();
   222→  await formatBtn.click();
   223→
   224→  // Button should show loading state
   225→  await expect(page.getByRole('button', { name: /formatting/i })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10_000 });
   226→
   227→  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page);
   228→
   229→  // If API key is missing, fail with a clear message
   230→  if (outcome === 'api_error') {
   231→    const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();
   232→    const hasApiKeyError = /api key is not configured|api key not configured|not configured/i.test(bodyText);
   233→    if (hasApiKeyError) {
   234→      throw new Error(
   235→        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: "OpenAI API key is not configured." ' +
   236→        'The Vercel deployment is missing the required AI API key environment variable. ' +
   237→        'AI formatting cannot function.'
   238→      );
   239→    }
   240→    throw new Error(`AI formatting returned an error. Page text: ${bodyText.substring(0, 300)}`);
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  expect(outcome, 'Formatting timed out after 90s').toBe('success');
   244→
   245→  // Name should be visible
   246→  await expect(page.getByText('Alex Rivera', { exact: false })).toBeVisible();
   247→
   248→  // No raw XML tags in visible content
   249→  const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();
   250→  expect(bodyText, 'Raw XML tags found in rendered preview').not.toMatch(/<\/?[a-z][^>]*>/);
   251→
   252→  // Key resume content should be preserved in the formatted output
   253→  expect(bodyText, 'Employer "Acme Corp" should be preserved in formatted output').toMatch(/Acme Corp/i);
   254→  expect(bodyText, 'Education should be preserved in formatted output').toMatch(/Berkeley|University of California/i);
   255→
   256→  // Preview should render HTML markup (headings, lists) — not just plain text
   257→  const pageHtml = await page.content();
   258→  const hasHtmlStructure = /<(h[1-6]|strong|b|ul|ol|li)\b/i.test(pageHtml);
   259→  expect(hasHtmlStructure, 'Formatted preview should render HTML structure (headings/lists), not plain text').toBe(true);
   260→
   261→  // Button should return to normal
   262→  await expect(page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 5_000 });
   263→});

    99→// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   100→
   101→/**
   102→ * Navigate to BASE_URL and wait for full hydration (including Nuxt 3 client-side
   103→ * mounting) before the test body begins.
   104→ */
   105→async function gotoAndWait(page: Page): Promise<void> {
   106→  await page.goto(BASE_URL);
   107→  await page.waitForLoadState('networkidle');
   108→  // Ensure the textarea is visible — confirms Vue has mounted
   109→  await page.locator('textarea').waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 15_000 });
   110→}
   111→
   112→/**
   113→ * Reliably fill a textarea and wait for Vue's reactive model to update.
   114→ * Uses click + fill + value verification to avoid intermittent fill() issues.
   115→ */
   116→async function fillTextarea(page: Page, text: string): Promise<void> {
   117→  const textarea = page.locator('textarea');
   118→  await textarea.click();
   119→  await textarea.fill(text);
   120→  await page.waitForTimeout(300);
   121→  // Verify the value was actually set; retry once if needed
   122→  const value = await textarea.inputValue();
   123→  if (value.length < 10 && text.length > 10) {
   124→    await textarea.click();
   125→    await textarea.fill(text);
   126→    await page.waitForTimeout(500);
   127→  }
   128→}
   129→
   130→/**
   131→ * Scope type-toggle buttons to the .type-selector container to avoid matching
   132→ * the "Format My Resume" / "Format My Letter" UButton, which also contains
   133→ * the words "Resume" and "Letter" in its accessible name.
   134→ */
   135→function getResumeToggle(page: Page) {
   136→  return page.locator('button.type-btn').filter({ hasText: 'Resume' });
   137→}
   138→
   139→function getLetterToggle(page: Page) {
   140→  return page.locator('button.type-btn').filter({ hasText: 'Letter' });
   141→}
   142→
   143→async function hasActiveClass(button: ReturnType<typeof getResumeToggle>): Promise<boolean> {
   144→  return button.evaluate(el => el.classList.contains('type-btn--active'));
   145→}
   146→

   105→          <p>Your formatted document will appear here.</p>

   111→              Try Resume Sample
   112→            </UButton>
   113→            <UButton variant="outline" size="sm" :disabled="isFormatting" @click="loadSample('letter')">
   114→              Try Letter Sample
   115→            </UButton>
   116→          </div>
   117→        </div>
   118→
   119→        <!-- Preview + review note -->
   120→        <template v-else>
   121→          <PreviewPanel
   122→            :xml-content="formattedXml"
   123→            :zoom="1"
   124→          />
   125→          <div class="review-note no-print">
   126→            Your content has been formatted but not rewritten. Please review before exporting.
   127→          </div>
   128→        </template>
   129→      </div>
   130→    </div>
   131→  </div>
   132→</template>
   133→
   134→<script setup lang="ts">
   135→import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   136→
   137→useHead({
   138→  title: 'OhMyDoc',
   139→})
   140→
   141→const placeholder = `Paste your resume or cover letter here.
   142→
   143→Example:
   144→Jane Smith
   145→jane@email.com · Toronto, ON
   146→
   147→Software Engineer with 8 years...`
   148→
   149→const textContent = ref('')
   150→const formattedXml = ref('')
   151→const isFormatting = ref(false)
   152→const formatError = ref('')
   153→const documentType = ref('')
   154→const divergence = ref(0)
   155→const validationMessage = ref('')
   156→const selectedDocType = ref<'resume' | 'letter'>('resume')
   157→
   158→const formatButtonLabel = computed(() =>
   159→  selectedDocType.value === 'letter' ? 'Format My Letter' : 'Format My Resume',
   160→)
   161→
   162→const showDivergenceWarning = computed(() => formattedXml.value && divergence.value > 0.05)
   163→
   164→function handlePrint() {
   165→  window.print()
   166→}
   167→
   168→async function loadSample(type: 'resume' | 'letter') {
   169→  const filename = type === 'resume' ? 'resume-sample.txt' : 'letter-sample.txt'
   170→  const response = await fetch(`/samples/${filename}`)
   171→  const text = await response.text()
   172→  textContent.value = text
   173→  selectedDocType.value = type
   174→  formatDocument()
   175→}
   176→
   177→async function formatDocument() {
   178→  validationMessage.value = ''
   179→
   180→  if (!textContent.value.trim()) return
   181→
   182→  if (textContent.value.trim().length < 50) {
   183→    validationMessage.value = 'Please paste at least 50 characters of content to format.'
   184→    return
   185→  }
   186→
   187→  if (isFormatting.value) return
   188→
   189→  isFormatting.value = true
   190→  formatError.value = ''
   191→  formattedXml.value = ''
   192→  documentType.value = ''
   193→  divergence.value = 0
   194→
   195→  try {
   196→    const result = await $fetch<{ xml: string, divergence: number, documentType: string }>('/api/format', {
   197→      method: 'POST',
   198→      body: { text: textContent.value, docType: selectedDocType.value },
   199→    })
   200→    formattedXml.value = result.xml
   201→    documentType.value = result.documentType
   202→    divergence.value = result.divergence
   203→  }
   204→  catch (err: unknown) {
   205→    const raw = (err as { data?: { rawResponse?: string } })?.data?.rawResponse
   206→    if (raw) {
   207→      console.error('[OhMyDoc] Raw AI response (malformed XML):', raw)
   208→    }
   209→    const message = (err as { data?: { message?: string } })?.data?.message
   210→    formatError.value = message || 'Something went wrong. Please try again.'
   211→  }
   212→  finally {
   213→    isFormatting.value = false
   214→  }
   215→}
